## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of current population P and time t, which is the canonical form of single-species population dynamics ODEs. The presence of both P and t suggests possible non-autonomous dynamics (time-varying parameters) or density-dependent growth.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (unlimited growth, no density dependence)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * P * (1 - c1 * P) (quadratic density dependence at low P)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (saturating per-capita growth)
- Logistic with harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (growth with proportional harvesting)
- Logistic with constant harvest: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant yield removal)
- Time-varying logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (seasonal carrying capacity)
- Exponential with seasonal forcing: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) (periodically varying growth rate)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * (c1 * P)**c2 (flexible asymmetric growth)
- Von Bertalanffy type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Power-law growth with decay: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P**c3 (generalized competing processes)
- Time-decaying growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(-c1 * t) (growth rate declining over time)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent regulation â†’ multiplicative factor (1 - P/K) or (1 - c*P) creating a nullcline at carrying capacity
- Allee effects (cooperative behavior at low density) â†’ additional multiplicative factor (P - threshold) creating an unstable equilibrium at low P
- Competing biological processes (anabolism vs catabolism) â†’ difference of power laws: c0*P^a - c1*P^b with different exponents
- Seasonal or periodic environmental forcing â†’ multiplicative modulation by (1 + c*sin(Ï‰*t)) on growth rate terms
- Per-capita growth rate declining with density â†’ dP/dt = P * f(P) where f is a decreasing function of P
- Multiple stable equilibria in population â†’ cubic or higher-order polynomial in P as the RHS
- Immigration/emigration as density-independent flux â†’ additive constant term independent of P in the growth equation
- Logarithmic density sensing (Gompertz-type) â†’ log(P) appearing in per-capita growth rate, giving asymmetric approach to equilibrium
- Resource depletion over time without explicit resource variable â†’ time-dependent decay factor exp(-c*t) or 1/(1+c*t) modulating growth
- Dormancy or delayed response â†’ dependence on t through non-periodic functions like polynomial or rational functions of t
